<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">South Korean association football player</div>

<table class="infobox" style="width: 22em"><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size: 125%; background-color: #b0c4de;">Son Heung-min</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hangul" title="Hangul">Hangul</a></th><td><div style="display:inline;font-size:1rem;"><span lang="ko-Hang" title="Korean-language text"></span></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hanja" title="Hanja">Hanja</a></th><td><div style="display:inline;font-size:1rem;"><span lang="ko-Hani" title="Korean-language text"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E5%AD%AB" class="extiw" title="wikt:"></a><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E8%88%88" class="extiw" title="wikt:"></a><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E6%85%9C" class="extiw" title="wikt:"></a></span></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Revised_Romanization_of_Korean" title="Revised Romanization of Korean">Revised Romanization</a></th><td><i lang="ko-Latn" title="Revised Romanization of Korean transliteration">Son Heungmin</i></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/McCune%E2%80%93Reischauer" title="McCune–Reischauer">McCune–Reischauer</a></th><td><i lang="ko-Latn" title="McCune–Reischauer transliteration">Son Hngmin</i></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Korean" title="Help:IPA/Korean">IPA</a></th><td><small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Korean" title="Help:IPA/Korean">[son x.min]</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Son Heung-min</b> (<a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a>: <span lang="ko"></span> <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="//: primary stress follows"></span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="//: &#39;o&#39; in &#39;body&#39;"></span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span></span><span class="wrap"> </span><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="//: primary stress follows"></span><span title="&#39;h&#39; in &#39;hi&#39;">h</span><span title="//: &#39;u&#39; in &#39;push&#39;"></span><span title="//: &#39;ng&#39; in &#39;sing&#39;"></span><span title="/./: syllable break">.</span><span title="&#39;m&#39; in &#39;my&#39;">m</span><span title="//: &#39;i&#39; in &#39;kit&#39;"></span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span></span>/</a></span></span>; born 8 July 1992) is a South Korean professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korean national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Position_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Position-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Widely regarded as one of the best wingers in the world and also one of the best Asian players in European football history, Son is often considered an icon in his home country and in Asia, and was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> in 2019, the highest-ever rank so far by an Asian player.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Son was also the first Asian player in history to score more than 50 goals in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Chuncheon" title="Chuncheon">Chuncheon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gangwon_Province,_South_Korea" title="Gangwon Province, South Korea">Gangwon Province</a>, Son joined <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a> at the age of 16 and debuted in the German <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> in 2010. In 2013, he moved to <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> for a club record €10&#160;million before signing for Tottenham for £22&#160;million two years later, becoming the most expensive Asian player in history.<sup id="cite_ref-AsianTransferRecord_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AsianTransferRecord-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> While at Tottenham, Son became the top Asian goalscorer in both Premier League and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> history,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and surpassed <a href="/wiki/Cha_Bum-kun" title="Cha Bum-kun">Cha Bum-kun</a>'s record for most goals scored by a Korean player in European competition.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-top_scorer_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-top_scorer-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> In 2019, he became the second Asian in history to reach and start a UEFA Champions League final after fellow countryman <a href="/wiki/Park_Ji-sung" title="Park Ji-sung">Park Ji-sung</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A full international since 2010, Son has represented South Korea at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a> and <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cups</a> and is his country's highest scorer in the World Cup jointly with Park Ji-sung and <a href="/wiki/Ahn_Jung-hwan" title="Ahn Jung-hwan">Ahn Jung-hwan</a> with three goals. Son has also represented South Korea at the <a href="/wiki/2018_Asian_Games" title="2018 Asian Games">2018 Asian Games</a>, where the team won gold, as well as the <a href="/wiki/2011_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2011 AFC Asian Cup">2011</a>, <a href="/wiki/2015_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2015 AFC Asian Cup">2015</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2019 AFC Asian Cup">2019</a> editions of the <a href="/wiki/AFC_Asian_Cup" title="AFC Asian Cup">AFC Asian Cup</a>. Korea was runner-up in 2015.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h2>
<p>Son Heung-min was born in <a href="/wiki/Chuncheon" title="Chuncheon">Chuncheon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gangwon_Province,_South_Korea" title="Gangwon Province, South Korea">Gangwon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11v11_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11v11-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> His father, <a href="/wiki/Son_Woong-jung" title="Son Woong-jung">Son Woong-jung</a> is a retired football player turned manager who once played for the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_B_team" title="South Korea national football B team">South Korea national football B team</a>.
</p><p>Son came through the <a href="/wiki/FC_Seoul_Reserves_and_Academy" title="FC Seoul Reserves and Academy">academy</a> at <a href="/wiki/FC_Seoul" title="FC Seoul">FC Seoul</a>, the same club that former Spurs defender <a href="/wiki/Lee_Young-pyo" title="Lee Young-pyo">Lee Young-pyo</a> played for.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Son was a <a href="/wiki/Ball_boy" title="Ball boy">ball boy</a> in an FC Seoul home match in 2008 when he was a FC Seoul youth player.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> At that time, his role model was midfielder <a href="/wiki/Lee_Chung-yong" title="Lee Chung-yong">Lee Chung-yong</a>, who played for <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bolton_Wanderers" class="mw-redirect" title="Bolton Wanderers">Bolton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Apart from his native language Korean, Son is also fluent in German and English. His agent Thies Bliemeister said Son was so determined to make himself a success in Europe that he learned German by watching episodes of <i><a href="/wiki/SpongeBob_SquarePants" title="SpongeBob SquarePants">SpongeBob SquarePants</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hamburger_SV">Hamburger SV</span></h3>
<p>In August 2008, Son dropped out of Dongbuk High School (formerly <a href="/wiki/FC_Seoul_Reserves_and_Academy" title="FC Seoul Reserves and Academy">FC Seoul U-18 Team</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and joined <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>'s youth academy at age 16 through <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%EB%8C%80%ED%95%9C%EC%B6%95%EA%B5%AC%ED%98%91%ED%9A%8C_%EC%9A%B0%EC%88%98%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98_%ED%95%B4%EC%99%B8%EC%9C%A0%ED%95%99_%ED%94%84%EB%A1%9C%EC%A0%9D%ED%8A%B8" class="extiw" title="ko:   ">Korean FA Youth Project</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> A year later, he returned to South Korea. After participating in the <a href="/wiki/2009_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2009 FIFA U-17 World Cup">FIFA U-17 World Cup</a>, he formally joined <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>'s youth academy in November 2009<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was impressive in the 2010–11 pre-season, leading the team with nine goals, and signed his first professional contract on his 18th birthday.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> After scoring against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in August, he was out for two months due to a foot injury. He returned on 30 October 2010 to score his first league goal, against <a href="/wiki/1._FC_K%C3%B6ln" title="1. FC Köln">1. FC Köln</a> in the 24th minute. The goal made Son the youngest <a href="/wiki/List_of_Hamburger_SV_players" title="List of Hamburger SV players">Hamburg player</a> to score a goal in the Bundesliga at 18, breaking the record held by <a href="/wiki/Manfred_Kaltz" title="Manfred Kaltz">Manfred Kaltz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Elia_son.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Elia_son.JPG/170px-Elia_son.JPG" decoding="async" width="170" height="207" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Elia_son.JPG/255px-Elia_son.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Elia_son.JPG/340px-Elia_son.JPG 2x" data-file-width="439" data-file-height="534" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Elia_son.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son (left) playing for Hamburger SV against <a href="/wiki/Eljero_Elia" title="Eljero Elia">Elia</a> of <a href="/wiki/Werder_Bremen" class="mw-redirect" title="Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> in August 2012</div></div></div>
<p>Son signed a new deal with Hamburg through 2014. Pundits said he had what it took to become the next <a href="/wiki/Cha_Bum-kun" title="Cha Bum-kun">Cha Bum-kun</a>, a legendary <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> forward and fellow South Korean.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Son scored three goals in 14 matches in all competition during the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Hamburger_SV_season" title="2010–11 Hamburger SV season">2010–11 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2010–11_season_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2010–11_season-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:197px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-Min.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Son_Heung-Min.jpg/195px-Son_Heung-Min.jpg" decoding="async" width="195" height="257" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Son_Heung-Min.jpg/292px-Son_Heung-Min.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Son_Heung-Min.jpg/390px-Son_Heung-Min.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1316" data-file-height="1736" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-Min.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son warming up for <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>During the 2011–12 pre-season, Son was explosive, scoring 18 times in only nine matches.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> After missing the opening match due to a fever, Son scored two goals within three matches.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 27 August, Son picked up an ankle injury in the 4–3 loss to 1. FC Köln and was initially projected to be out of action for four to six weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> His recovery was quicker than expected and he returned to action only three weeks later as a substitute in a 1–0 loss against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a> on 17 September. Over the course of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Hamburger_SV_season" title="2011–12 Hamburger SV season">2011–12 season</a>, he made 30 appearances for Hamburg and scored five goals,<sup id="cite_ref-2011–12_season_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2011–12_season-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> including crucial goals against <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a> and <a href="/wiki/1._FC_N%C3%BCrnberg" title="1. FC Nürnberg">1. FC Nürnberg</a> at the end of the season to help ensure that Hamburg remained in the Bundesliga.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following Hamburger SV's 2012–13 offseason moves, which saw the transfers of the team's strikers <a href="/wiki/Mladen_Petri%C4%87" title="Mladen Petri">Mladen Petri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Guerrero" title="Paolo Guerrero">Paolo Guerrero</a> to <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sport_Club_Corinthians_Paulista" title="Sport Club Corinthians Paulista">Corinthians</a> respectively, manager <a href="/wiki/Thorsten_Fink" title="Thorsten Fink">Thorsten Fink</a> chose to name Son a starter. The <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Bundesliga" title="2012–13 Bundesliga">2012–13 season</a> was a breakthrough season for Son as he scored two goals in an away fixture against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> on 9 February 2013, helping his team to a 4–1 victory. Son was chosen <i>Mann des Tages (Man of the Match)</i> by <a href="/wiki/Kicker_(sports_magazine)" title="Kicker (sports magazine)"><i>kicker</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> On 14 April, Son netted two goals in a 2–1 win against <a href="/wiki/1._FSV_Mainz_05" title="1. FSV Mainz 05">Mainz 05</a>. He finished the season with 12 goals, becoming the fifth South Korean footballer to achieve double digits in goals in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Hamburger_SV_season" title="2012–13 Hamburger SV season">2012–13 season</a> with 12 goals in 34 matches in all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-2012–13_season_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2012–13_season-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bayer_Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:285px;"><a href="/wiki/File:LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90,_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_(1).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90%2C_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_%281%29.jpg/425px-LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90%2C_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_%281%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90%2C_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_%281%29.jpg/566px-LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90%2C_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_%281%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="1272" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:LG%EC%A0%84%EC%9E%90,_%EB%A0%88%EB%B2%84%EC%BF%A0%EC%A0%A0%EA%B3%BC_%E2%80%98%EC%B0%A9%ED%95%9C%E2%80%99_%EC%8A%A4%ED%8F%AC%EC%B8%A0%EB%A7%88%EC%BC%80%ED%8C%85_%ED%8E%BC%EC%B3%90_(1).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son playing for <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 13 June 2013, <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> confirmed Son's transfer for reportedly €10&#160;million, which was the highest transfer fee in the club's history at the time. He agreed to a five-year deal with the team.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Son adjusted quickly to his new club in the pre-season, scoring three goals in his first three appearances for the team in exhibition matches (against <a href="/wiki/TSV_1860_Munich" title="TSV 1860 Munich">1860 Munich</a>, <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a> and <a href="/wiki/KAS_Eupen" class="mw-redirect" title="KAS Eupen">KAS Eupen</a> respectively).<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 November 2013, Son scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> for Leverkusen in a 5–3 win against his former club Hamburgers SV.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On 7 December, Son scored a crucial goal against Borussia Dortmund to put his club just four points off the summit of the Bundesliga. On 10 May 2014, Son scored another goal against <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> ensuring his team a spot for the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League">2014–15 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Bayer_04_Leverkusen_season" title="2013–14 Bayer 04 Leverkusen season">2013–14 season</a> with 12 goals in 43 matches.<sup id="cite_ref-2013–14_season_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013–14_season-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Son scored a hat-trick against <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">VfL Wolfsburg</a> on 14 February 2015, in a 4–5 defeat, scoring when they were losing 0–3.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Bayer_04_Leverkusen_season" title="2014–15 Bayer 04 Leverkusen season">2014–15 season</a> with 17 goals in 42 matches.<sup id="cite_ref-2014–15_season_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014–15_season-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Son started the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Bayer_04_Leverkusen_season" title="2015–16 Bayer 04 Leverkusen season">2015–16 season</a> with Bayer Leverkusen. He made a league appearance<sup id="cite_ref-2015-16_season_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015-16_season-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and a <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">Champions League qualifying</a> match.<sup id="cite_ref-Heung-min_Son_»_Club_matches_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Heung-min_Son_»_Club_matches-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tottenham_Hotspur">Tottenham Hotspur</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span></h4>
<p>On 28 August 2015, Son joined <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> for £22&#160;million (€30&#160;million) on a five-year contract, subject to work permit and international clearance.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Upon his signing, he became the most expensive Asian player in football history.<sup id="cite_ref-AsianTransferRecord_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AsianTransferRecord-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> The record had been held since 2001 by Japanese <a href="/wiki/Hidetoshi_Nakata" title="Hidetoshi Nakata">Hidetoshi Nakata</a>, who transferred from <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> to <a href="/wiki/Parma_Calcio_1913" title="Parma Calcio 1913">Parma</a> for €25&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Son made his debut on 13 September away to <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a>, being replaced by <a href="/wiki/Andros_Townsend" title="Andros Townsend">Andros Townsend</a> in the 62nd minute of a 1–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> In Tottenham's first match of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Europa League">2015–16 UEFA Europa League</a> on 17 September, Son netted his first two goals for the club in a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Qaraba%C4%9F_FK" title="Qaraba FK">Qaraba FK</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored his first Premier League goal, against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> at <a href="/wiki/White_Hart_Lane" title="White Hart Lane">White Hart Lane</a>, netting in the 68th minute to give Tottenham their first home Premier League win of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 28 December in the match against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>, Son replaced <a href="/wiki/Tom_Carroll_(English_footballer)" title="Tom Carroll (English footballer)">Tom Carroll</a> in the 80th minute and scored Tottenham's winning goal in the 89th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On 2 May, he scored the second goal against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in a crucial match to give Spurs hope of winning the Premier League. Chelsea equalised in the second half, however, handing over the title to <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:233px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg/231px-Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg" decoding="async" width="231" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg/346px-Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg/461px-Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg 2x" data-file-width="825" data-file-height="787" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-min_2016.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son playing for <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> on a game against PFC CSKA Moscow in 2016.</div></div></div>
<p>Before the season, he reportedly asked Spurs manager <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_Pochettino" title="Mauricio Pochettino">Mauricio Pochettino</a> for permission to leave Tottenham in an attempt to get more playing time, but was instead given a chance to fight for his place at Spurs.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 10 September 2016, Son scored two goals and created a third in his first appearance of the season, in a 4–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Son followed that performance up with a second brace, coming at <a href="/wiki/Middlesbrough_F.C." title="Middlesbrough F.C.">Middlesbrough</a> on 24 September, earning his team a 1–2 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Upon equalling his league goal total from the previous season in 25 fewer matches, Son was hailed by Pochettino as "a different person – he's more mature and he knows the league and he's settled in fantastically now."<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Son continued his excellent run of form with his fifth goal in five matches on 27 September in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>. Playing at <a href="/wiki/PFC_CSKA_Moscow" title="PFC CSKA Moscow">CSKA Moscow</a>, Son slipped a shot past goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Igor_Akinfeev" title="Igor Akinfeev">Igor Akinfeev</a> for the only goal of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> On 14 October, Son was named the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> for September, being the first South Korean and first Asian to receive the award.<sup id="cite_ref-POTM_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POTM-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the Christmas break Son continued to score the odd goal over the following couple of months and then on 12 March 2017 he scored his first Spurs hat trick in the FA Cup against <a href="/wiki/Millwall_F.C." title="Millwall F.C.">Millwall</a> in a 6–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> In the same match, he was racially abused by a section of the Millwall fans who chanted "DVD" and "he's selling three for a fiver" whenever he touched the ball, referencing a stereotype towards east Asians.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> He scored in the 2–0 victory away at <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a> on 1 April 2017,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> and four days later he scored in the 91st minute to put Spurs ahead at Swansea, in a game where they were losing 1–0 after 88 minutes and ended up winning 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> A brace at home to Watford the following weekend brought his season total to 18 goals, 11 in the Premier League, his best ever goals return.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 12 May 2017, Tottenham announced that Son had won the Premier League Player of the Month for April, the second time of his career and thus becoming the only player in 2016–17 to win the award 2 times.<sup id="cite_ref-april-POM_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-april-POM-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 18 May 2017, Son bagged a brace away to <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> as part of a 6–1 rout of their former title rivals. With 21 goals in all competitions, Son joined <a href="/wiki/Harry_Kane" title="Harry Kane">Harry Kane</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dele_Alli" title="Dele Alli">Dele Alli</a> as the first trio of Spurs players with over 20 goals on the season.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span></h4>
<p>Son scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2017–18 season</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> game against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> on 13 September 2017 at Spurs temporary home <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>, which Spurs won 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first Premier League goal in the season when Spurs beat <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> 4–1 at home.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 5 November 2017, Son scored the only goal in the 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>. The goal brought his tally in the Premier League to 20 and in doing so he became the top Asian goalscorer in Premier League history, breaking the record set by <a href="/wiki/Park_Ji-Sung" class="mw-redirect" title="Park Ji-Sung">Park Ji-Sung</a> at <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-top_scorer_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-top_scorer-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> On 13 January 2018, Son scored a goal and provided an assist in a game against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>, matching the club record set in 2004 by <a href="/wiki/Jermain_Defoe" title="Jermain Defoe">Jermain Defoe</a> of scoring in five consecutive home games.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> On 28 February 2018, Son scored a brace and assisted <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Llorente" title="Fernando Llorente">Fernando Llorente</a> as Tottenham beat <a href="/wiki/Rochdale_A.F.C" class="mw-redirect" title="Rochdale A.F.C">Rochdale</a> 6–1 in the 5th Round of the FA Cup. Son also converted a penalty, but his goal was overruled by the <a href="/wiki/Video_assistant_referee" title="Video assistant referee">video assistant referee</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Son has become the first Asian to finish the season as a top-10 goal scorer in the English Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span></h4>
<p>On 20 July 2018, Son signed a new five-year deal extending his contract with Tottenham until 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> The first goals of the season came in October 2018 when he scored a brace in his 150th game for Tottenham in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_EFL_Cup" title="2018–19 EFL Cup">2018–19 EFL Cup</a> match against West Ham.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first league goal in the season, his 50th goal for the club in all competitions, in a solo effort in the 3–1 home win against Chelsea, inflicting the first defeat for Chelsea in the Premier League this season.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> This goal won the Premier League's Goal of the Month award for November.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> On 13 February 2019, Son scored the first goal in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>, in the first leg of the round of 16, <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the month he was named Premier League Player of the Year at the London Football Awards.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> On 3 April 2019, Son scored the very first professional goal at the new <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_Stadium" title="Tottenham Hotspur Stadium">Tottenham Hotspur Stadium</a> in a 2–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 April 2019, Son scored the very first European competition goal at the Tottenham Hotspur Stadium in a 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> in the quarterfinals of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">2018–19 Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> In the return leg, Son scored twice to earn Tottenham a 4–4 aggregate win on the <a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">away goals rule</a> and help the club reach the semi-finals of the competition for the first time since 1962, and only the second time ever. His brace also saw him become the highest scoring Asian player in the history of the tournament with 12 goals, overtaking the previous record holder, <a href="/wiki/Maxim_Shatskikh" class="mw-redirect" title="Maxim Shatskikh">Maxim Shatskikh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 4 May 2019, Son received his first red card in the Premier League due to his vindictive action against <a href="/wiki/Jefferson_Lerma" title="Jefferson Lerma">Jefferson Lerma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span></h4>
<p>Son opened his 2019–20 account on 14 September 2019 by scoring two goals against Crystal Palace in the Premier League with a final result of 4–0.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> On 21 October, Son was named in the 30-man shortlist for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2019 Ballon d&#39;Or">2019 Ballon d'Or</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 3 November, Son was sent off during a 1–1 draw with Everton after sliding into <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9_Gomes" title="André Gomes">André Gomes</a> from behind, causing him to fall awkwardly and suffer a severe ankle injury. The injury prompted great concern and anguish from the players and supporters; Son was visibly highly distressed by the incident.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Following a red card for a challenge on Gomes, Son also received suspension for three Premier League games.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> However, many professionals including former Everton player Kevin Kilbane expressed criticism of the red card decision, and Tottenham made an appeal to the Football Association against the dismissal. The FA accepted the appeal and Son's red card was rescinded on 5 November.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Three days after this incident, in a 4–0 Champions League away game to <a href="/wiki/Red_Star_Belgrade" title="Red Star Belgrade">Red Star Belgrade</a>, in which Son scored a brace, rather than celebrating his first goal, he apologised to the camera for what happened at <a href="/wiki/Goodison_Park" title="Goodison Park">Goodison Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 23 November 2019, Son scored Tottenham's first goal with <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> as manager, earning him <a href="/wiki/Man-of-the-match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man-of-the-match">Man-of-the-match</a> in a 3–2 Spurs victory against West Ham.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> On 7 December, in the match against <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>, Son ran from one end of the pitch to the other, going past seven Burnley players, to score an individual goal that was immediately labelled a goal of the season contender. The nature of the goal saw Mourinho dub him "Sonaldo Nazario" in reference to the type of goal former Brazilian international <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> would score.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> In January 2020, Son was awarded the Premier League goal of the month for December for his goal against Burnley,<sup id="cite_ref-Premier_League_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Premier_League-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> eventually winning him the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Goal_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Goal of the Season">Goal of the Season</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-PLGOTS_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PLGOTS-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>  The goal was further recognised by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> with a <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Pusk%C3%A1s_Award" title="FIFA Puskás Award">Puskás Award</a> as the best goal of the past 12 months in December 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 December 2019, facing Chelsea, Son was sent off after raising his boot against <a href="/wiki/Antonio_R%C3%BCdiger" title="Antonio Rüdiger">Antonio Rüdiger</a>'s ribs.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> On 16 February 2020, Son scored two goals at Villa Park and earned a 3–2 victory for Tottenham, in which he became the first Asian footballer to score 50 goals in the Premier League, with 51 scored goals in 151 Premier League matches.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> Son played the full game despite suffering a fracture to his arm at the 31st second of the game.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Head coach José Mourinho declared at a later stage that he was not optimistic regarding Son's injury and that it was likely that the South Korean would be sidelined for the rest of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 April 2020, while football was suspended due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Europe" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Europe">COVID-19 pandemic in Europe</a>, it was confirmed that Son would carry out his mandatory military service for South Korea.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> After completing a two-week quarantine on his return to Korea, he served with the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Korea_Marine_Corps" title="Republic of Korea Marine Corps">Marine Corps</a> for three weeks on <a href="/wiki/Jeju_Island" title="Jeju Island">Jeju Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span></h4>
<p>In the second Premier League match of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2020–21 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2020–21 season</a>, Son scored four goals, all assisted by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Kane" title="Harry Kane">Harry Kane</a>, in a 5–2 win against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> and the first League win of the season. This was the first time in Premier League history in which a single player scored four goals in a match while being assisted by the same teammate.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>  In the Premier League game on 4 October, he scored a brace against Manchester United to help Tottenham win 6–1, which is the biggest win for Tottenham at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> and their best result against United since a home win in 1932.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Based on his performances, Son received his third Premier League Player of the Month award on 13 November 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 January 2021, Son scored his 100th goal for Tottenham in the 3–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> On 10 February 2021, he provided three assists, but Tottenham lost 5–4 to <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_FA_Cup" title="2020–21 FA Cup">FA Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> On 7 March, Son provided an assist to Harry Kane in a 4–1 win against Crystal Palace, and this, their 14th combined goal effort whereby one assisted another, set a record for the most goal combinations in a single Premier League season.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_and_2011_Asian_Cup">Youth and 2011 Asian Cup</span></h3>
<p>Son was a member of the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_under-17_football_team" title="South Korea national under-17 football team">South Korea national team</a> that participated at the <a href="/wiki/2009_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2009 FIFA U-17 World Cup">2009 FIFA U-17 World Cup</a> held in Nigeria.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> He scored 3 goals in this tournament.
</p><p>On 24 December 2010, Son was named in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea national team</a>'s squad for the <a href="/wiki/2011_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2011 AFC Asian Cup">2011 AFC Asian Cup</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> making his debut for the national team in a pre-tournament friendly against <a href="/wiki/Syria_national_football_team" title="Syria national football team">Syria</a> on 30 December.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> At the tournament finals, Son scored his first international goal during a 4–1 group stage defeat of <a href="/wiki/India_national_football_team" title="India national football team">India</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup">2014 World Cup</span></h3>
<p>On 7 October 2011, after initially missing the first two matches of South Korea's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(AFC)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (AFC)">2014 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> campaign on 2 and 6 September 2011 due to an ankle injury, Son played in a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game#Association_football" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> against <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_football_team" title="Poland national football team">Poland</a>, and was again featured in 11 October World Cup qualifier against the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates_national_football_team" title="United Arab Emirates national football team">United Arab Emirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> His selection for national team play was a point of concern for Son's father, however, who caused a stir by asking the Korea Football Association not to select his son for the national team in the immediate future so he can rest and mature more as a player. <a href="/wiki/Cho_Kwang-rae" title="Cho Kwang-rae">Cho Kwang-rae</a>, then the South Korea head coach, responded by saying that he would continue to call up Son when needed.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_(51).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg/220px-2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg/330px-2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg/440px-2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_%2851%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4912" data-file-height="3264" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2013.09.06_Korea_Rep._vs_Haiti_(51).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son being interviewed after playing for <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>Son turned down the opportunity to participate in the <a href="/wiki/2012_London_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="2012 London Olympics">2012 London Olympics</a>, opting to concentrate on his club career at Hamburger SV. Son was quoted as saying, "In Korea, an Olympic appearance has a special meaning, but I want to speed up for Hamburg. What matters is to pour all my time into team training."<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Son did, however, play for the national team in the autumn of 2012 for two <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(AFC)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (AFC)">2014 FIFA World Cup qualifiers</a> against <a href="/wiki/Lebanon_national_football_team" title="Lebanon national football team">Lebanon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iran_national_football_team" title="Iran national football team">Iran</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> and became a regular call-up in friendlies and World Cup qualifying matches in 2013. In the World Cup qualifier against <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_football_team" title="Qatar national football team">Qatar</a> on 23 March 2013, Son came on as a substitute in the 81st minute and scored the winning goal in the 96th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In June 2014, Son was named in South Korea's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> On 22 June, he scored in a 4–2 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> in the team's second group match.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Korea_Football_Association" title="Korea Football Association">Korea Football Association</a> requested Bayer Leverkusen to allow Son to play in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Asian_Games" title="2014 Asian Games">2014 Asian Games</a>, as winning the gold medal at the tournament would grant Son exemption from military service. Despite Son affirming his interest and the KFA's efforts, his club at the time, Bayer Leverkusen, refused to release him, as his absence would mean the team would lose him for at least six matches.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2015_Asian_Cup">2015 Asian Cup</span></h3>
<p>Son was selected for South Korea for the <a href="/wiki/2015_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2015 AFC Asian Cup">2015 AFC Asian Cup</a> in Australia. At the quarter-final stage, he scored both of the team's goals in the 2–0 extra time defeat of <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan_national_football_team" title="Uzbekistan national football team">Uzbekistan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2015_AFC_Asian_Cup_Final" title="2015 AFC Asian Cup Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_soccer_team" title="Australia national soccer team">the hosts</a>, he equalised in added time, but his team lost 2–1 after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-Asian_Cup_final_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Asian_Cup_final-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> He was chosen as one of three forwards in the Team of the Tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-AC2015_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AC2015-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2016_Summer_Olympics">2016 Summer Olympics</span></h3>
<p>In June 2016, Son was named as an over-age player in South Korea's squad for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2016 Summer Olympics</a>. Son amassed two goals in the group stages with a goal against <a href="/wiki/Fiji_national_under-23_football_team" title="Fiji national under-23 football team">Fiji</a> and another against <a href="/wiki/Germany_Olympic_football_team" title="Germany Olympic football team">Germany</a>, helping his team to top the group with two wins and a draw. South Korea was eliminated by <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_under-23_football_team" title="Honduras national under-23 football team">Honduras</a> in the quarterfinals, with Son missing crucial chances.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span></h3>
<p>On 3 September 2015 at the <a href="/wiki/Hwaseong_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Hwaseong Stadium">Hwaseong Stadium</a>, Son scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in an 8–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Laos_national_football_team" title="Laos national football team">Laos</a> in <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_AFC_Second_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – AFC Second Round">the second round</a> of <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">qualification</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 June 2017, Son broke his right forearm after falling awkwardly on his arm during a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_AFC_Third_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – AFC Third Round">World Cup qualifier</a> match in Doha against <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_football_team" title="Qatar national football team">Qatar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> He was part of the team that saw Korea qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> after a 0–0 draw against <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</a> on 5 September 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> On 4 June 2018, Son was selected in <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#South_Korea" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">23-man squad</a> for the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 23 June, Son scored a goal from outside the penalty area – a curling strike into the top corner – though his side was defeated with a 2–1 loss to <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a> in their second group stage match of the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> On 27 June, during their final group stage match, he scored the second goal in the 97th minute in their 2–0 victory over world champions <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>, sealing their elimination.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_Asian_Games">2018 Asian Games</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:197px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg/195px-Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg" decoding="async" width="195" height="246" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg/292px-Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg/389px-Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg 2x" data-file-width="428" data-file-height="541" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Son_Heung-min_at_2019_AFC_Asian_Cup.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Son playing for South Korea at <a href="/wiki/2019_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2019 AFC Asian Cup">2019 AFC Asian Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>Son was selected as one of three overage players permitted in the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_under-23_football_team" title="South Korea national under-23 football team">under-23 team</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2018_Asian_Games_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2018 Asian Games – Men&#39;s tournament">football event</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2018_Asian_Games" title="2018 Asian Games">2018 Asian Games</a> in Indonesia.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> He captained the team in the final game of the group stage against <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan_national_under-23_football_team" title="Kyrgyzstan national under-23 football team">Kyrgyzstan</a>, scoring the only goal of the match to help the team reach the knockout rounds.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> He also captained the team in the knockout rounds and reached the final after the Taeguk Warriors beat <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_national_under-23_football_team" title="Vietnam national under-23 football team">Vietnam</a>, 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> In the gold medal match, Son assisted in both extra-time goals in a 2–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_under-23_football_team" title="Japan national under-23 football team">Japan</a>, which guaranteed the entire squad's exemption from <a href="/wiki/Conscription_in_South_Korea" title="Conscription in South Korea">mandatory military service</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2019_Asian_Cup">2019 Asian Cup</span></h3>
<p>Son was called up as <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2019_AFC_Asian_Cup" title="2019 AFC Asian Cup">2019 AFC Asian Cup</a> in the United Arab Emirates by <a href="/wiki/Paulo_Bento" title="Paulo Bento">Paulo Bento</a>, but missed the first two group matches due to an agreement with Tottenham Hotspur related to his call-up.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> He recorded an assist in the third group game against <a href="/wiki/China_national_football_team" title="China national football team">China</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> However, his play at the tournament was lethargic due to lack of physical strength in his busy schedule,<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> and he returned to London following his team's defeat in the quarter-finals to the eventual champion <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_football_team" title="Qatar national football team">Qatar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h2>
<p>Son can basically play in any attacking position,<sup id="cite_ref-Position_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Position-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> (<a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">winger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">second striker</a>, <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a>) and can even be deployed as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> or <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Wing-back" title="Defender (association football)">wing-back</a> if necessary. He himself has confirmed this, saying, "I don't care where I play. The main thing is I'm in the game. I can play as a second striker or behind. Whatever the coach says, I'll do. I don't have a favorite position. I'll be anywhere and always on the throttle."<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_players_in_Premier_League_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_players_in_Premier_League-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Son is known for his two-footed ability, explosive pace, positional sense, movement, close control and clinical finishing which make him especially effective on the counter-attack.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, he has drawn praise from teammates and in the media for his selfless work-rate and defensive contribution, and is capable of providing assists for teammates, in addition to scoring goals himself.<sup id="cite_ref-best_players_in_Premier_League_152-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_players_in_Premier_League-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sponsorship_and_media">Sponsorship and media</span></h2>
<p>Son has a sponsorship deal with sportswear and equipment supplier <a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<p>Son has stated that he does not intend to marry until after he retires from football. He has dated the <a href="/wiki/K-pop" title="K-pop">K-pop</a> singers <a href="/wiki/Bang_Min-ah" title="Bang Min-ah">Bang Min-ah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yoo_So-young" title="Yoo So-young">Yoo So-young</a>, and is currently single.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Son used the suspension of football during the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a> to complete <a href="/wiki/Conscription_in_South_Korea" title="Conscription in South Korea">South Korean mandatory military service</a>. He was exempted from military service with a gold medal at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2018_Asian_Games" title="Football at the 2018 Asian Games">Asian Games</a>, but he had to do basic military training regardless of exemption. He completed basic training in the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Korea_Marine_Corps" title="Republic of Korea Marine Corps">Republic of Korea Marine Corps</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jeju_Province" title="Jeju Province">Jeju</a> in April–May 2020, finishing in the top five of 157 trainees.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
